Monk finished with 17 points and was 4-for-10 on 3-pointers.,Westbrook, acquired in an offseason trade, had 15 points in the final quarter and overtime to eclipse his previous high of 15 points with the Lakers.,''That's why we felt great about this move,'' Vogel said. ''Last year we lost LeBron and A.D. for a long stretch, and we didn't have enough to sustain throughout the regular season and win in the playoffs.
